  1  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE add_contact
  2  ( pv_member_id         NUMBER
  3  , pv_contact_type      NUMBER
  4  , pv_last_name         VARCHAR2
  5  , pv_first_name        VARCHAR2
  6  , pv_middle_name       VARCHAR2 := NULL
  7  , pv_address_type      NUMBER   := NULL
  8  , pv_street_address    STREET_ADDRESS_TABLE := street_address_table()
  9  , pv_city              VARCHAR2 := NULL
 10  , pv_state_province    VARCHAR2 := NULL
 11  , pv_postal_code       VARCHAR2 := NULL
 12  , pv_country_code      VARCHAR2 := NULL
 13  , pv_telephone_type    NUMBER   := NULL
 14  , pv_area_code         VARCHAR2 := NULL
 15  , pv_telephone_number  VARCHAR2 := NULL
 16  , pv_created_by        NUMBER
 17  , pv_creation_date     DATE     := SYSDATE
 18  , pv_last_updated_by   NUMBER
 19  , pv_last_update_date  DATE     := SYSDATE) IS
 20  
 21    -- Define a local variable because an address may not be provided.
 22    lv_address_id     NUMBER;
 23  
 24  BEGIN
 25  
 26    -- Set savepoint to guarantee all or nothing happens.
 27    SAVEPOINT add_contact;
 28  
 29    -- Insert into contact table.
 30    INSERT INTO contact
 31    ( contact_id
 32    , member_id
 33    , contact_type
 34    , last_name
 35    , first_name
 36    , middle_name
 37    , created_by
 38    , creation_date
 39    , last_updated_by
 40    , last_update_date )
 41    VALUES
 42    ( contact_s1.NEXTVAL
 43    , pv_member_id
 44    ,(SELECT   common_lookup_id
 45      FROM     common_lookup
 46      WHERE    common_lookup_table = 'CONTACT'
 47      AND      common_lookup_column = 'CONTACT_TYPE'
 48      AND      common_lookup_type = 'CUSTOMER') -- pv_contact_type)
 49    , pv_last_name
 50    , pv_first_name
 51    , pv_middle_name
 52    , pv_created_by
 53    , pv_creation_date
 54    , pv_last_updated_by
 55    , pv_last_update_date );
 56  
 57    -- Check conditions before inserting an address.
 58    IF pv_address_type IS NOT NULL   AND
 59       pv_city IS NOT NULL           AND
 60       pv_state_province IS NOT NULL AND
 61       pv_postal_code IS NOT NULL    THEN
 62  
 63       INSERT INTO address
 64       VALUES
 65       ( address_s1.nextval
 66       , contact_s1.currval
 67       , pv_address_type
 68       , pv_city
 69       , pv_state_province
 70       , pv_postal_code
 71       , pv_created_by
 72       , pv_creation_date
 73       , pv_last_updated_by
 74       , pv_last_update_date);
 75  
 76       -- Preserve primary key for reuse as a foreign key.
 77       -- -------------------------------------------------------------
 78       -- Oracle 11g Forward supports this syntax.
 79       -- -------------------------------------------------------------
 80       lv_address_id := address_s1.currval;
 81  
 82       -- Preserve primary key for reuse as a foreign key.
 83       -- -------------------------------------------------------------
 84       -- Oracle 10g Backward Compatibility uses this syntax.
 85       -- -------------------------------------------------------------
 86       -- SELECT address_s1.currval INTO lv_address_id FROM dual;
 87  
 88      -- Check conditions before inserting a street address.
 89      IF pv_street_address.COUNT > 0 THEN
 90        FOR i IN 1..pv_street_address.COUNT LOOP
 91  
 92          INSERT INTO street_address VALUES
 93          ( street_address_s1.nextval
 94          , lv_address_id
 95          , i
 96          , pv_street_address(i)
 97          , pv_created_by
 98          , pv_creation_date
 99          , pv_last_updated_by
100          , pv_last_update_date);
101  
102        END LOOP;
103      END IF;
104  
105    END IF;
106  
107    -- Check condidtions before inserting a telephone.
108    IF pv_telephone_type IS NOT NULL AND
109       pv_country_code IS NOT NULL AND
110       pv_area_code IS NOT NULL AND
111       pv_telephone_number IS NOT NULL THEN
112  
113      INSERT INTO telephone VALUES
114      ( telephone_s1.nextval
115      , contact_s1.currval
116      , lv_address_id           -- Reuse the foreign key if available.
117      , pv_telephone_type
118      , pv_country_code
119      , pv_area_code
120      , pv_telephone_number
121      , pv_created_by
122      , pv_creation_date
123      , pv_last_updated_by
124      , pv_last_update_date);
125  
126    END IF;
127  
128  EXCEPTION
129  
130    WHEN others THEN
131      ROLLBACK TO add_contact;
132      RAISE_APPLICATION_ERROR(-20001,SQLERRM);
133  
134* END add_contact;

  1  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE add_member
  2  ( pv_membership_type    VARCHAR2 := 'GROUP'
  3  , pv_account_number     VARCHAR2
  4  , pv_credit_card_number VARCHAR2
  5  , pv_credit_card_type   VARCHAR2 := 'VISA_CARD'
  6  , pv_contact_type       VARCHAR2 := 'CUSTOMER'
  7  , pv_contact_list       CONTACT_LIST_TYPE
  8  , pv_address_type       VARCHAR2 := 'HOME'
  9  , pv_st_addr1           VARCHAR2 := NULL
 10  , pv_st_addr2           VARCHAR2 := NULL
 11  , pv_st_addr3           VARCHAR2 := NULL
 12  , pv_city               VARCHAR2 := NULL
 13  , pv_state_province     VARCHAR2 := NULL
 14  , pv_postal_code        VARCHAR2 := NULL
 15  , pv_country_code       VARCHAR2 := NULL
 16  , pv_telephone_type     VARCHAR2 := 'HOME'
 17  , pv_area_code          VARCHAR2 := NULL
 18  , pv_telephone_number   VARCHAR2 := NULL
 19  , pv_created_by         NUMBER
 20  , pv_creation_date      DATE     := SYSDATE
 21  , pv_last_updated_by    NUMBER
 22  , pv_last_update_date   DATE     := SYSDATE) IS
 23  
 24    -- Declare surrogate key variables.
 25    lv_member_id         NUMBER;
 26    lv_member_type       NUMBER;
 27    lv_credit_card_type  NUMBER;
 28  
 29    -- Declare a null collection until you can evaluate element values.
 30    lv_street_address    STREET_ADDRESS_TABLE := street_address_table();
 31  
 32    -- Declare local function to get type.
 33    FUNCTION get_type
 34    ( table_name  VARCHAR2
 35    , column_name VARCHAR2
 36    , type_name   VARCHAR2) RETURN NUMBER IS
 37      retval NUMBER;
 38    BEGIN
 39      SELECT   common_lookup_id
 40      INTO     retval
 41      FROM     common_lookup
 42      WHERE    common_lookup_table = table_name
 43      AND      common_lookup_column = column_name
 44      AND      common_lookup_type = type_name;
 45      RETURN retval;
 46    END get_type;
 47  
 48  BEGIN
 49  
 50    -- Initialize local street address array for all not null values.
 51    FOR i IN 1..3 LOOP
 52      lv_street_address.EXTEND;
 53      IF    pv_st_addr1 IS NOT NULL THEN
 54        lv_street_address(i) := pv_st_addr1;
 55      ELSIF pv_st_addr2 IS NOT NULL THEN
 56        lv_street_address(i) := pv_st_addr2;
 57      ELSIF pv_st_addr3 IS NOT NULL THEN
 58        lv_street_address(i) := pv_st_addr3;
 59      END IF;
 60    END LOOP;
 61  
 62    -- Set savepoint to guarantee all or nothing happens.
 63    SAVEPOINT add_member;
 64  
 65    -- Select sequence by using Oracle 10g and backward methods.
 66    SELECT  member_s1.nextval
 67    INTO    lv_member_id
 68    FROM    dual;
 69  
 70    -- Declare types based on local function that can't run in SQL context.
 71    lv_member_type := get_type('MEMBER','MEMBER_TYPE',pv_membership_type);
 72    lv_credit_card_type := get_type('MEMBER','CREDIT_CARD_TYPE',pv_credit_card_type);
 73  
 74    INSERT INTO member
 75    ( member_id
 76    , member_type
 77    , account_number
 78    , credit_card_number
 79    , credit_card_type
 80    , created_by
 81    , creation_date
 82    , last_updated_by
 83    , last_update_date)
 84    VALUES
 85    ( lv_member_id
 86    , lv_member_type
 87    , pv_account_number
 88    , pv_credit_card_number
 89    , lv_credit_card_type
 90    , pv_created_by
 91    , pv_creation_date
 92    , pv_last_updated_by
 93    , pv_last_update_date);
 94  
 95    -- Call contact for as many as exist.
 96    FOR i IN 1..pv_contact_list.COUNT LOOP
 97  
 98      -- Call procedure to insert records in related tables.
 99      add_contact(
100        pv_member_id => lv_member_id
101      , pv_contact_type => get_type('CONTACT','CONTACT_TYPE',pv_contact_type)
102      , pv_first_name => pv_contact_list(i).first_name
103      , pv_middle_name => pv_contact_list(i).middle_name
104      , pv_last_name => pv_contact_list(i).last_name
105      , pv_address_type => get_type('ADDRESS','ADDRESS_TYPE',pv_address_type)
106      , pv_street_address => lv_street_address
107      , pv_city => pv_city
108      , pv_state_province => pv_state_province
109      , pv_postal_code => pv_postal_code
110      , pv_telephone_type => get_type('TELEPHONE','TELEPHONE_TYPE',pv_telephone_type)
111      , pv_country_code => pv_country_code
112      , pv_area_code => pv_area_code
113      , pv_telephone_number => pv_telephone_number
114      , pv_created_by => pv_created_by
115      , pv_last_updated_by => pv_last_updated_by);
116  
117    END LOOP;
118  
119    -- Write all records from both procedures.
120    COMMIT;
121  
122  EXCEPTION
123    WHEN others THEN
124      ROLLBACK TO add_member;
125      RAISE_APPLICATION_ERROR(-20002,SQLERRM);
126* END add_member;
